    FROM [carts] AS [c]
    WHERE [c].[UserModelId] = @__userId_0 AND [c].[MyStatus] = 0
) AS [c1]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c0].[Id], [c0].[CartId], [c0].[GiftModelId], [c0].[Quantity], [g].[Id] AS [Id0], [g].[CategoryModelId], [g].[Description], [g].[DonorModelId], [g].[Image], [g].[Name], [g].[TicketPrice], [g].[UserModelId], [g].[isRaffleDone]
    FROM [cartItems] AS [c0]
    INNER JOIN [gifts] AS [g] ON [c0].[GiftModelId] = [g].[Id]
) AS [s] ON [c1].[Id] = [s].[CartId]
ORDER BY [c1].[Id], [s].[Id]

    SELECT TOP(1) [d].[Id], [d].[Email], [d].[FirstName], [d].[LastName], [d].[Phone]
    FROM [donors] AS [d]
    WHERE [d].[Id] = @__id_0
) AS [d0]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [g].[Id], [g].[CategoryModelId], [g].[Description], [g].[DonorModelId], [g].[Image], [g].[Name], [g].[TicketPrice], [g].[UserModelId], [g].[isRaffleDone], [c].[Id] AS [Id0], [c].[Name] AS [Name0]

) AS [s] ON [d0].[Id] = [s].[DonorModelId]
